    [0m[94masync[39;49;00m [94mdef[39;49;00m[90m [39;49;00m[92mwait_for[39;49;00m(fut, timeout):[90m[39;49;00m
    [90m    [39;49;00m[33m"""Wait for the single Future or coroutine to complete, with timeout.[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m

    [90m    [39;49;00m[33m"""Block until the internal flag is true.[39;49;00m
